Macro to calculate address of an aliased word in the peripheral bitband area for a peripheral register and bit (bit band region 0x40000000 to 0x400\+FFFFF). 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Reg} & Register to access. \\
\hline
{\em Bit} & Bit number to access. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Address of the aliased word in the peripheral bitband area. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
